---
title: "Linux内核数据结构（链表、队列、红黑树）"
date: 2022-06-17 08:41:31
categories:
  - linux
---

<p><span style="color:#444444;font-family:&#39;Open Sans&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;font-size:14px;font-style:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;background-color:#ffffff;display:inline !important;float:none;"><a target="_blank" href="http://woofy.cn/2016/11/19/kernel_data_structures_1/" rel="noreferrer">http://woofy.cn/2016/11/19/kernel_data_structures_1/</a></span></p>
<footer class="entry-meta" style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;vertical-align:baseline;display:block;clear:both;line-height:1.84615;color:#757575;font-family:&#39;Open Sans&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;font-style:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;background-color:#ffffff;"><footer class="entry-meta" style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;vertical-align:baseline;display:block;clear:both;line-height:1.84615;color:#757575;font-family:&#39;Open Sans&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;font-style:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;background-color:#ffffff;"><div class="entry-content" style="margin:0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;color:#444444;font-family:&#39;Open Sans&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;font-style:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;background-color:#ffffff;">
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;">Linux和其他大型软件项目一样，需要用到各种各样的数据结构.<br>在内核场景下，对数据结构的实现主要有以下几点要求：<br>1) 高性能：作为内核基本库一定要快.<br>2) 通用性：内核开发者尽可能复用，不重复造轮子防止膨胀.<br>3) 易用性：接口和参数尽量少，用法明确.<br>4) 安全性：主要指并发访问等，本文暂不关注.<br>在这几点的综合考虑权衡下，c语言的内核的相关实现都有其独特的地方.<br>本文从内核中使用最广的链表(list)、队列(fifo)、红黑树三种结构出发快速考察体验一番.</p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;"></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;">一、链表</strong></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;">链表list是内核中最简单和使用最多的，早期的做法是每人都为自己的链表类型实现一套操作.<br>为了不重复开发尽可能使用同一套，现在内核单独把链表抽象成了源码级插件，如果开发者需要，<br>仅需将内核链表节点插入到自己的结构体中，就可以将其<strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;">变为</strong>链表类型.<br>链表节点中的指针不是指向wrapper结构体地址，而是指向相邻的链表节点.</p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;"></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;">这样做有几个好处：<br>a) 大家都用同一套链表节点定义，因而可以提供统一的链表操作函数.<br>b) 链表核心结构与用户数据无关，达到了通用(generic).<br>c) 系统无关，空间分配由上层负责，本身是纯逻辑模块.<br>d) 使用上扩展起来也更加灵活，比如让同一个实体处于多套链表中只需为其添加链接节点.</p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;"></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;">具体举例：</p>
<div style="margin:0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;">
<div class="syntaxhighlighter cpp" style="margin:1em 0px !important;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:1em !important;vertical-align:baseline;width:625px;position:relative !important;overflow: !important;background-color:#ffffff !important;">

!important;box-sizing: !important;font-weight:normal !important;font-style:normal !important;box-shadow:none !important;display:inline !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</code><code class="cpp comments" style="margin:0px !important;padding:0px !important;border:0px !important;font-size:1em !important;vertical-align:baseline !important;font-family:Monaco, Consolas, &#39;Bitstream Vera Sans Mono&#39;, &#39;Courier New&#39;, Courier, monospace !important;line-height:1.1em !important;border-radius:0px !important;background:none !important;bottom:auto !important;float:none !important;height:auto !important;left:auto !important;overflow:visible !important;position:static !important;right:auto !important;text-align:left !important;top:auto !important;width:auto !important;box-sizing: !important;font-weight:normal !important;font-style:normal !important;box-shadow:none !important;display:inline !important;color:#008200 !important;">//...</code></div>
<div class="line number20 index19 alt1" style="margin:0px !important;padding:0px 1em !important;border:0px !important;font-size:1em !important;vertical-align:baseline !important;border-radius:0px !important;background:#FFFFFF none !important;bottom:auto !important;float:none !important;height:auto !important;left:auto !important;line-height:1.1em !important;overflow:visible !important;position:static !important;right:auto !important;text-align:left !important;top:auto !important;width:auto !important;box-sizing: !important;font-family:Monaco, Consolas, &#39;Bitstream Vera Sans Mono&#39;, &#39;Courier New&#39;, Courier, monospace !important;font-weight:normal !important;font-style:normal !important;box-shadow:none !important;white-space:pre !important;"><code class="cpp plain" style="margin:0px !important;padding:0px !important;border:0px !important;font-size:1em !important;vertical-align:baseline !important;font-family:Monaco, Consolas, &#39;Bitstream Vera Sans Mono&#39;, &#39;Courier New&#39;, Courier, monospace !important;line-height:1.1em !important;border-radius:0px !important;background:none !important;bottom:auto !important;float:none !important;height:auto !important;left:auto !important;overflow:visible !important;position:static !important;right:auto !important;text-align:left !important;top:auto !important;width:auto !important;box-sizing: !important;font-weight:normal !important;font-style:normal !important;box-shadow:none !important;display:inline !important;color:#000000 !important;">};</code></div>
</div>
</td>
</tr></tbody></table></div>

<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;">从定义看linux的list本质上是带头结点的双向循环链表.<br>这种链表的实现可以非常精简高效,头结点作为哨兵结点避免了一些边界情况的判断：<br>一个链表如果存在，即使为空，也至少包含一个头结点.</p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;"></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;">上面task_struct中真正作为链接器节点的是sibling（task本身作为子进程），children只是指向其子进程链表（task本身作为父亲）.<br>具体而言，链表节点(list_head)在使用上分为两种：<br>1. 作为内嵌到用户结构体中的桩，其wrapper struct一定是链表中的数据结点.<br>2. 作为链表头结点指针，其wrapper struct与链表数据一般没有关系，仅持有对链表的引用.</p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;"></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;">作图说明：</p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;"></p>
<div class="wp-caption alignnone" style="margin: 0px; padding: 4px; border: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; max-width: 100%; width: 1494px;"><img src="./Linux内核数据结构（链表、队列、红黑树） - KM平台_files/cos-file-url(1)" alt="" style="position: relative; z-index: 2;" class="amplify"><br><p class="wp-caption-text" style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:2;font-style:italic;color:#757575;">task_sliblings</p>
</div>
<br>如图所示，sibling是将孩子们串到一起的第1类链接节点，位于所有<strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;">子进程</strong>task_struct中；<br>children是<strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;">父进程</strong>task_struct中指向该链表的指针，只是恰好也放在了task_struct里.</div>
<div class="entry-content" style="margin:0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;color:#444444;font-family:&#39;Open Sans&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;font-style:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;background-color:#ffffff;">
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;"></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;">最后linux提供了一组编译宏方便我们直接在用户结构体层面进行操作，如以下遍历子进程的代码：</p>
<div style="margin:0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;">

Vera Sans Mono&#39;, &#39;Courier New&#39;, Courier, monospace !important;font-weight:normal !important;font-style:normal !important;box-shadow:none !important;white-space:pre !important;"><code class="cpp spaces" style="margin:0px !important;padding:0px !important;border:0px !important;font-size:1em !important;vertical-align:baseline !important;font-family:Monaco, Consolas, &#39;Bitstream Vera Sans Mono&#39;, &#39;Courier New&#39;, Courier, monospace !important;line-height:1.1em !important;border-radius:0px !important;background:none !important;bottom:auto !important;float:none <div class="line number7 index6 alt2" style="margin:0px !important;padding:0px 1em !important;border:0px !important;font-size:1em !important;vertical-align:baseline !important;border-radius:0px !important;background:#FFFFFF none !important;bottom:auto !important;float:none !important;height:auto !important;left:auto !important;line-height:1.1em !important;overflow:visible !important;position:static !important;right:auto !important;text-align:left !important;top:auto !important;width:auto !important;box-sizing: !important;font-family:Monaco, Consolas, &#39;Bitstream Vera Sans Mono&#39;, &#39;Courier New&#39;, Courier, monospace !important;font-weight:normal !important;font-style:normal !important;box-shadow:none !important;white-space:pre !important;"><code class="cpp plain" style="margin:0px !important;padding:0px !important;border:0px !important;font-size:1em !important;vertical-align:baseline !important;font-family:Monaco, Consolas, &#39;Bitstream Vera Sans Mono&#39;, &#39;Courier New&#39;, Courier, monospace !important;line-height:1.1em !important;border-radius:0px !important;background:none !important;bottom:auto !important;float:none !important;height:auto !important;left:auto !important;overflow:visible !important;position:static !important;right:auto !important;text-align:left !important;top:auto !important;width:auto !important;box-sizing: !important;font-weight:normal !important;font-style:normal !important;box-shadow:none !important;display:inline !important;color:#000000 !important;">}</code></div>
</div>
</td>
</tr></tbody></table></div>

<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;">链表适合数据量不大的遍历场景；用链表也可以实现栈和队列.</p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;"></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;">二、队列</strong><br>kfifo本质上是个循环队列，空间连续总大小固定，每个元素类型大小一致，<br>适合容量比较明确的一些生产-消费者场景.<br>因为无需操作指针，比链表实现的队列更高效.<br>队列的空间可以由内核初始化时从kmalloc分配，也可以用户指定.<br>队列大小(元素个数size)会被调整为<strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;">2的幂次</strong>（原因下面会说）.</p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;"></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;">kfifo核心定义：</p>
<div style="margin:0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;">

!important;overflow:visible !important;position:static !important;right:auto !important;text-align:left !important;top:auto !important;width:auto !important;box-sizing: !important;font-weight:normal !important;font-style:normal !important;box-shadow:none !important;display:inline !important;color:#008200 !important;">//出队列（队头）虚拟指针，只增，小于等于in，指向下一个出队元素</code></div>
<div class="line number4 index3 alt1" style="margin:0px !important;padding:0px 1em !important;border:0px !important;font-size:1em !important;vertical-align:baseline !important;border-radius:0px <div class="line number6 index5 alt1" style="margin:0px !important;padding:0px 1em !important;border:0px !important;font-size:1em !important;vertical-align:baseline !important;border-radius:0px <div class="line number7 index6 alt2" style="margin:0px !important;padding:0px 1em !important;border:0px !important;font-size:1em !important;vertical-align:baseline !important;border-radius:0px !important;background:#FFFFFF none !important;bottom:auto !important;float:none !important;height:auto !important;left:auto !important;line-height:1.1em !important;overflow:visible !important;position:static !important;right:auto !important;text-align:left !important;top:auto !important;width:auto !important;box-sizing: !important;font-family:Monaco, Consolas, &#39;Bitstream Vera Sans Mono&#39;, &#39;Courier New&#39;, Courier, monospace !important;font-weight:normal !important;font-style:normal !important;box-shadow:none !important;white-space:pre !important;"><code class="cpp plain" style="margin:0px !important;padding:0px !important;border:0px !important;font-size:1em !important;vertical-align:baseline !important;font-family:Monaco, Consolas, &#39;Bitstream Vera Sans Mono&#39;, &#39;Courier New&#39;, Courier, monospace !important;line-height:1.1em !important;border-radius:0px !important;background:none !important;bottom:auto !important;float:none !important;height:auto !important;left:auto !important;overflow:visible !important;position:static !important;right:auto !important;text-align:left !important;top:auto !important;width:auto !important;box-sizing: !important;font-weight:normal !important;font-style:normal !important;box-shadow:none !important;display:inline !important;color:#000000 !important;">};</code></div>
</div>
</td>
</tr></tbody></table></div>

<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;">kfifo的实现也很精炼，有几个特点：<br>a) in和out本身是只增的，并且始终保持 in&gt;=out.<br>当in==out时队列为空，in-out==size时队列满.</p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;"></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;">b) 在需要时才将in和out映射到实际位置（效果同取摸）<br>为了更快采用位运算即如 in &amp; mask的方式.</p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;"></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;">mask是根据元素个数事先算好的：mask = size - 1. 这就是为什么要求size为2的幂.</p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;"></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;">再来看a)中队列为空和队列为满的条件，一般的循环队列为了区分队列为空和队列为满这两种情况，<br>需要浪费一个元素的空间，而内核的循环队列可以把<strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;">空间全部利用上，没有任何浪费</strong>.<br>其原因在于in和out的表示，不必始终指向真实位置，而是采用虚拟指针方式，始终自增，从不绕回；<br>在需要计算实际地址的时候才使用mask临时做映射，判断队列状态只需用in和out之差.<br>这样就不存在冲突问题了，因为队列为空和为满回到了其原本的判定方式.</p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; line-height: 1.71429;"><br>作图说明：<br><img src="./Linux内核数据结构（链表、队列、红黑树） - KM平台_files/cos-file-url(2)" alt="" style="position: relative; z-index: 2;" class="amplify"><br>可以看到，in总是比out大，其差值是当前队列元素个数，这和队列原始逻辑视图是一致的.</p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;"></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;">需要时再做映射，这样处理本质上是<strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;">缩小用于work-around的特殊实现部分的范围</strong>.<br>参考入队列的代码：</p>
<div style="margin:0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;">

!important;background:#FFFFFF none !important;bottom:auto !important;float:none !important;height:auto !important;left:auto !important;line-height:1.1em !important;overflow:visible !important;position:static !important;right:auto !important;text-align:left !important;top:auto !important;width:auto !important;box-sizing: !important;font-family:Monaco, Consolas, &#39;Bitstream Vera Sans Mono&#39;, &#39;Courier New&#39;, Courier, monospace !important;font-weight:normal !important;font-style:normal !important;box-shadow:none !important;white-space:pre !important;"><code class="cpp spaces" style="margin:0px !important;padding:0px !important;border:0px !important;font-size:1em !important;vertical-align:baseline !important;font-family:Monaco, Consolas, &#39;Bitstream Vera Sans Mono&#39;, &#39;Courier New&#39;, Courier, monospace !important;line-height:1.1em !important;border-radius:0px !important;background:none !important;bottom:auto !important;float:none !important;box-sizing: !important;font-weight:normal !important;font-style:normal !important;box-shadow:none !important;display:inline !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</code><code class="cpp plain" style="margin:0px !important;padding:0px !important;border:0px !important;font-size:1em <div class="line number16 index15 alt1" style="margin:0px !important;padding:0px 1em !important;border:0px !important;font-size:1em !important;vertical-align:baseline !important;border-radius:0px !important;background:#FFFFFF none !important;bottom:auto !important;float:none !important;height:auto !important;left:auto !important;line-height:1.1em !important;overflow:visible !important;position:static !important;right:auto !important;text-align:left !important;top:auto !important;width:auto !important;box-sizing: !important;font-family:Monaco, Consolas, &#39;Bitstream Vera Sans Mono&#39;, &#39;Courier New&#39;, Courier, monospace !important;font-weight:normal !important;font-style:normal !important;box-shadow:none !important;white-space:pre !important;">&nbsp;</div>

<div class="line number19 index18 alt2" style="margin:0px !important;padding:0px 1em !important;border:0px !important;font-size:1em !important;vertical-align:baseline !important;border-radius:0px class="cpp plain" style="margin:0px !important;padding:0px !important;border:0px !important;font-size:1em !important;vertical-align:baseline !important;font-family:Monaco, Consolas, &#39;Bitstream <div class="line number20 index19 alt1" style="margin:0px !important;padding:0px 1em !important;border:0px !important;font-size:1em !important;vertical-align:baseline !important;border-radius:0px !important;background:#FFFFFF none !important;bottom:auto !important;float:none !important;height:auto !important;left:auto !important;line-height:1.1em !important;overflow:visible !important;position:static !important;right:auto !important;text-align:left !important;top:auto !important;width:auto !important;box-sizing: !important;font-family:Monaco, Consolas, &#39;Bitstream Vera Sans Mono&#39;, &#39;Courier New&#39;, Courier, monospace !important;font-weight:normal !important;font-style:normal !important;box-shadow:none !important;white-space:pre !important;"><code class="cpp plain" style="margin:0px !important;padding:0px !important;border:0px !important;font-size:1em !important;vertical-align:baseline !important;font-family:Monaco, Consolas, &#39;Bitstream Vera Sans Mono&#39;, &#39;Courier New&#39;, Courier, monospace !important;line-height:1.1em !important;border-radius:0px !important;background:none !important;bottom:auto !important;float:none !important;height:auto !important;left:auto !important;overflow:visible !important;position:static !important;right:auto !important;text-align:left !important;top:auto !important;width:auto !important;box-sizing: !important;font-weight:normal !important;font-style:normal !important;box-shadow:none !important;display:inline !important;color:#000000 !important;">}</code></div>
</div>
</td>
</tr></tbody></table></div>

<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;">三、红黑树</strong></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;"></strong></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;">红黑树是一种自平衡的二叉查找树，内核中主要用于大量元素高效查找和动态更新的场景，如CFS调度、epoll等.</p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;"><br>红黑树通过维护以下若干特性来保持树的大致平衡：<br>1) 每个节点要么是红色，要么是黑色.<br>2) 树根节点是黑色.<br>3) 叶子节点不含数据，且为黑色.<br>4) 红色节点的子节点必为黑色.<br>5) 从树根到任意一叶子节点的路径上的黑色节点个数都相同.<br>注意4)蕴含了红色结点的父节点必为黑色；5)蕴含了其对红黑树的任意子树也成立.<br>另外任意黑节点为根的子树是红黑树；红节点为根的子树将其根染黑后也是红黑树.</p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;"></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;">以上第4和5点可以保证根到叶子的最长路径不超过最短路径的2倍，因而是大致平衡的（树高h&lt;2lg(n+1)）.<br>为什么一定是这一批性质呢，这是由Sedgewick等教授精细设计的（最早从某类B树启发，见wiki）.<br>设计目标是使得在插入、删除等修改场景下对这些性质（即树的平衡）的维护代价尽量小（虽然编程实现不简单），均摊复杂度为O(1). 而作为对比，AVL是高度平衡的，左右子树最多相差一层，对查找而言更高效，但插入、删除等修改操作下对其维护代价更大，算法复杂度为O(lg(n)).<br>因此如果数据集合是静态的则适合用AVL树，因为只用build一遍；而内核场景状态是快速变化的，显然红黑树更适用.</p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;"></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;">具体如何维护这些性质呢，简单来说，就是当搜索树发生了插入、删除等操作后，如果有性质被破坏（意味可能已失衡），通过搜索树的基本旋转操作（调整两边树高），加上相关节点颜色的改变等措施，总能使性质得到恢复.</p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;"></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;">具体算法参考Wiki<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rbtree" style="margin:0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;color:#9f9f9f;">Rbtree</a>，linux基本是按此实现的.<br>linux红黑树的使用和实现有以下几个特点：<br>a) 和list一样，通过内嵌红黑树节点rb_node到宿主结构体的方式来灵活支持rb树的引入.<br>b) 提供了插入、删除后的动态平衡调整接口，但不提供查找过程，需使用者自己实现.<br>c) 在时间和空间上处理细节非常高效到位，特别是前者，后面举例说明.</p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;"></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;">不提供查找是因为元素的比较逻辑由其宿主数据决定，而树节点本身和链表一样是key无关的，<br>因此只能通过回调的方式来实现通用的查找操作，但linux主要从性能角度出发不鼓励使用回调，<br>而是交给开发者自己实现高效查找，好在二叉树查找本身结构很简单，虽然可能会引入一些重复代码.<br>这里的本质问题是通用性（generic）和高性能上一般不可兼顾，特别对于c语言而言.<br>（链表list能做到是因为其上的操作与用户数据无关，除了指针的指向，而linux也将其解决了）</p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;"></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;">树节点的定义：</p>
<div style="margin:0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;">

<div class="line number17 index16 alt2" style="margin:0px !important;padding:0px 1em !important;border:0px !important;font-size:1em !important;vertical-align:baseline !important;border-radius:0px !important;background:#FFFFFF none !important;bottom:auto !important;float:none !important;height:auto !important;left:auto !important;line-height:1.1em !important;overflow:visible !important;position:static !important;right:auto !important;text-align:left !important;top:auto !important;width:auto !important;box-sizing: !important;font-family:Monaco, Consolas, &#39;Bitstream Vera Sans Mono&#39;, &#39;Courier New&#39;, Courier, monospace !important;font-weight:normal !important;font-style:normal !important;box-shadow:none !important;white-space:pre !important;"><code class="cpp plain" style="margin:0px !important;padding:0px !important;border:0px !important;font-size:1em !important;vertical-align:baseline !important;font-family:Monaco, Consolas, &#39;Bitstream Vera Sans Mono&#39;, &#39;Courier New&#39;, Courier, monospace !important;line-height:1.1em !important;border-radius:0px !important;background:none !important;bottom:auto !important;float:none !important;height:auto !important;left:auto !important;overflow:visible !important;position:static !important;right:auto !important;text-align:left !important;top:auto !important;width:auto !important;box-sizing: !important;font-weight:normal !important;font-style:normal !important;box-shadow:none !important;display:inline !important;color:#000000 !important;">}</code></div>
</div>
</td>
</tr></tbody></table></div>

<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;">这里看到一个省空间的普遍做法是，由于结构体里都是long类型，整体也是按long做内存地址对齐的，即地址的最后2个bit一定是0，于是parent指针可以同时也用来存color（只需1个bit）. 所以rb_parent宏取实际父节点地址时要把后2个bit给mask掉.</p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;"></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;">另一个细节是在一些场景下，可以事先知道当前节点的颜色，比如新插入节点根据算法一定是红色，而红色bit为0，因此取其parent时不需要mask，于是专门有一个rb_red_parent内部函数优化处理，即不做mask直接返回.</p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;"></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;">红黑树insert调整算法相对简单，可以浏览下linux的实现：</p>
<div style="margin:0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;">

!important;display:inline !important;color:#000000 !important;">} </code><code class="cpp keyword bold" style="margin:0px !important;padding:0px !important;border:0px !important;font-size:1em !important;display:inline !important;color:#006699 !important;">else</code> <code class="cpp plain" style="margin:0px !important;padding:0px !important;border:0px !important;font-size:1em <div class="line number90 index89 alt1" style="margin:0px !important;padding:0px 1em !important;border:0px !important;font-size:1em !important;vertical-align:baseline !important;border-radius:0px class="cpp spaces" style="margin:0px !important;padding:0px !important;border:0px !important;font-size:1em !important;vertical-align:baseline !important;font-family:Monaco, Consolas, &#39;Bitstream !important;font-weight:normal !important;font-style:normal !important;box-shadow:none !important;display:inline !important;color:#008200 !important;">//对称处理，略.</code></div>
<div class="line number91 index90 alt2" style="margin:0px !important;padding:0px 1em !important;border:0px !important;font-size:1em !important;vertical-align:baseline !important;border-radius:0px <div class="line number92 index91 alt1" style="margin:0px !important;padding:0px 1em !important;border:0px !important;font-size:1em !important;vertical-align:baseline !important;border-radius:0px <div class="line number93 index92 alt2" style="margin:0px !important;padding:0px 1em !important;border:0px !important;font-size:1em !important;vertical-align:baseline !important;border-radius:0px !important;background:#FFFFFF none !important;bottom:auto !important;float:none !important;height:auto !important;left:auto !important;line-height:1.1em !important;overflow:visible !important;position:static !important;right:auto !important;text-align:left !important;top:auto !important;width:auto !important;box-sizing: !important;font-family:Monaco, Consolas, &#39;Bitstream Vera Sans Mono&#39;, &#39;Courier New&#39;, Courier, monospace !important;font-weight:normal !important;font-style:normal !important;box-shadow:none !important;white-space:pre !important;"><code class="cpp plain" style="margin:0px !important;padding:0px !important;border:0px !important;font-size:1em !important;vertical-align:baseline !important;font-family:Monaco, Consolas, &#39;Bitstream Vera Sans Mono&#39;, &#39;Courier New&#39;, Courier, monospace !important;line-height:1.1em !important;border-radius:0px !important;background:none !important;bottom:auto !important;float:none !important;height:auto !important;left:auto !important;overflow:visible !important;position:static !important;right:auto !important;text-align:left !important;top:auto !important;width:auto !important;box-sizing: !important;font-weight:normal !important;font-style:normal !important;box-shadow:none !important;display:inline !important;color:#000000 !important;">}</code></div>
</div>
</td>
</tr></tbody></table></div>

<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;">这里代码还是很精简的，但已经可以开始看出临时变量复用的趋势了；尤其是到了delete调整的代码里（未贴出），由于算法本身也更复杂，临时变量复用得也较多，需要从局部细节和整体一起着手理解，毕竟作者应该也是仔细推敲后精细构造的代码；总之总体感受就是细节处很精致，但也牺牲了一定的直观性.</p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;"></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;">四、其他</strong><br>内核中其他数据结构如map(idr)、radix-tree、bitmap、B+树等使用场景相对较少，部分与系统耦合，后面遇到了再分享.</p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;"></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;">五、小结</strong><br>数据结构和算法原理都是一样的，而linus说过对内核来说"It's all about the details."<br>在保证良好的通用性、易用性的前提下，内核能把这些工具实现得比任何教科书伪码都更加精炼和极其高效，确实是集体智慧的精彩舞台.</p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;"></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;">参考资料：<br>1. Robert Love《Linux Kernel Development》3rd, chapter 6.<br>2. Linux-4.8.7</p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px;padding:0px;border:0px;font-size:14px;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:1.71429;"></p>
